392→ */\n   393→function loadProjectDetails(projectId) {\n   394→    fetch(`https://${window.location.host}/${db}/report/5977?JSON_KV&FR_ПроектID=${projectId}`)\n   395→        .then(response => response.json())\n   396→        .then(data => {\n   397→            projectDetails = data;\n   398→            displayTasksAndOperations(data);\n   399→        })\n   400→        .catch(error => {\n   401→            console.error('Error loading project details:', error);\n   402→            alert('Ошибка загрузки задач проекта');\n   403→        });\n   404→}\n   405→\n   406→/**\n   407→ * Display tasks and operations\n   408→ */\n   409→function displayTasksAndOperations(data) {\n   410→    const taskList = document.getElementById('taskList');\n   411→    if (!taskList) return;\n   412→\n   413→    if (data.length === 0) {\n   414→        taskList.innerHTML = '<div style=\"padding: 20px; text-align: center; color: #6c757d;\">Задачи не найдены</div>';\n   415→        return;\n   416→    }\n   417→\n   418→    // Group by tasks\n   419→    const taskGroups = {};\n   420→    data.forEach(item => {\n   421→        const taskId = item['Задача проектаID'];\n   422→        if (!taskGroups[taskId]) {\n   423→            taskGroups[taskId] = {\n   424→                task: item,\n   425→                operations: []\n   426→            };\n   427→        }\n   428→        if (item['ОперацияID']) {\n   429→            taskGroups[taskId].operations.push(item);\n   430→        }\n   431→    });\n   432→\n   433→    // Sort tasks by order\n   434→    const sortedTaskIds = Object.keys(taskGroups).sort((a, b) => {\n   435→        const orderA = parseInt(taskGroups[a].task['Задача проектаOrder'] || 0);\n   436→        const orderB = parseInt(taskGroups[b].task['Задача проектаOrder'] || 0);\n   437→        return orderA - orderB;\n   438→    });\n   439→\n   440→    taskList.innerHTML = sortedTaskIds.map((taskId, index) => {\n   441→        const group = taskGroups[taskId];\n   442→        const task = group.task;\n   443→        const operations = group.operations.sort((a, b) => {\n   444→            const orderA = parseInt(a['ОперацияOrder'] || 0);\n   445→            const orderB = parseInt(b['ОперацияOrder'] || 0);\n   446→            return orderA - orderB;\n   447→        });\n   448→\n   449→        let html = `\n   450→            <div class=\"task-item\" draggable=\"true\" data-task-id=\"${taskId}\" data-order=\"${task['Задача проектаOrder']}\">\n   451→                <span class=\"drag-handle\">☰</span>\n   452→                <span class=\"task-order\">${index + 1}</span>\n   453→                <div class=\"task-content\">\n   454→                    <strong>${escapeHtml(task['Задача проекта'] || 'Без названия')}</strong>\n   455→                    ${task['Задача Описание'] ? '<br><small>' + escapeHtml(task['Задача Описание']) + '</small>' : ''}\n   456→                    ${task['Статус задачи'] ? '<br><small>Статус: ' + escapeHtml(task['Статус задачи']) + '</small>' : ''}\n   457→                </div>\n   458→                <div class=\"task-actions\">\n   459→                    <button class=\"btn btn-sm btn-primary\" onclick=\"showAddOperationModal('${taskId}')\">+ Операция</button>\n   460→                    <button class=\"btn btn-sm btn-secondary\" onclick=\"editTask('${taskId}')\">Изм.</button>\n   461→                </div>\n   462→            </div>\n   463→        `;\n   464→\n   465→        // Add operations\n   466→        operations.forEach((op, opIndex) => {\n   467→            if (op['ОперацияID']) {\n   468→                html += `\n   469→                    <div class=\"operation-item\" draggable=\"true\" data-operation-id=\"${op['ОперацияID']}\" data-order=\"${op['ОперацияOrder']}\">\n   470→                        <span class=\"drag-handle\">☰</span>\n   471→                        <span class=\"operation-order\">${opIndex + 1}</span>\n   472→                        <div class=\"operation-content\">\n   473→                            ${escapeHtml(op['Операция'] || 'Без названия')}\n   474→                            ${op['Операция Начать'] ? '<br><small>Начать: ' + escapeHtml(op['Операция Начать']) + '</small>' : ''}\n   475→                            ${op['Операция Кол-во'] ? '<br><small>Кол-во: ' + escapeHtml(op['Операция Кол-во']) + ' ' + escapeHtml(op['Операция Ед.изм.'] || '') + '</small>' : ''}\n   476→                        </div>\n   477→                        <div class=\"operation-actions\">\n   478→                            <button class=\"btn btn-sm btn-secondary\" onclick=\"editOperation('${op['ОперацияID']}')\">Изм.</button>\n   479→                        </div>\n   480→                    </div>\n   481→                `;\n   482→            }\n   483→        });\n   484→\n   485→        return html;\n   486→    }).join('');\n   487→\n   488→    // Add drag and drop handlers\n   489→    addDragAndDropHandlers();\n   490→}\n   491→\n   492→/**\n   493→ * Add drag and drop handlers for reordering\n   494→ */\n   495→function addDragAndDropHandlers() {\n   496→    const tasks = document.querySelectorAll('.task-item');\n   497→    const operations = document.querySelectorAll('.operation-item');\n   498→\n   499→    tasks.forEach(task => {\n   500→        task.addEventListener('dragstart', handleDragStart);\n   501→        task.addEventListener('dragover', handleDragOver);\n   502→        task.addEventListener('drop', handleDrop);\n   503→        task.addEventListener('dragend', handleDragEnd);\n   504→    });\n   505→\n   506→    operations.forEach(operation => {\n   507→        operation.addEventListener('dragstart', handleDragStart);\n   508→        operation.addEventListener('dragover', handleDragOver);\n   509→        operation.addEventListener('drop', handleDrop);\n   510→        operation.addEventListener('dragend', handleDragEnd);\n   511→    });\n   512→}\n   513→\n   514→let draggedElement = null;\n   515→\n   516→function handleDragStart(e) {\n   517→    draggedElement = this;\n   518→    this.classList.add('dragging');\n   519→    e.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'move';\n   520→\n   521→    // Console tracing for drag start\n   522→    const isTask = this.classList.contains('task-item');\n   523→    const id = isTask ? this.dataset.taskId : this.dataset.operationId;\n   524→    console.log(`[DRAG] Start: ${isTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${id}, Order=${this.dataset.order}`);\n   525→}\n   526→\n   527→function handleDragOver(e) {\n   528→    if (e.preventDefault) {\n   529→        e.preventDefault();\n   530→    }\n   531→    e.dataTransfer.dropEffect = 'move';\n   532→\n   533→    // Console tracing for drag over (throttled to avoid spam)\n   534→    if (!this._lastDragOverLog || Date.now() - this._lastDragOverLog > 500) {\n   535→        const isTask = this.classList.contains('task-item');\n   536→        const id = isTask ? this.dataset.taskId : this.dataset.operationId;\n   537→        console.log(`[DRAG] Over: ${isTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${id}`);\n   538→        this._lastDragOverLog = Date.now();\n   539→    }\n   540→\n   541→    return false;\n   542→}\n   543→\n   544→function handleDrop(e) {\n   545→    if (e.stopPropagation) {\n   546→        e.stopPropagation();\n   547→    }\n   548→\n   549→    console.log('[DRAG] Drop event triggered');\n   550→\n   551→    // Check if both elements are of the same type (both tasks or both operations)\n   552→    const isDraggedTask = draggedElement.classList.contains('task-item');\n   553→    const isDraggedOperation = draggedElement.classList.contains('operation-item');\n   554→    const isDropTargetTask = this.classList.contains('task-item');\n   555→    const isDropTargetOperation = this.classList.contains('operation-item');\n   556→    const isSameType = (isDraggedTask && isDropTargetTask) || (isDraggedOperation && isDropTargetOperation);\n   557→\n   558→    if (draggedElement !== this && isSameType) {\n   559→        const draggedId = isDraggedTask ? draggedElement.dataset.taskId : draggedElement.dataset.operationId;\n   560→        const dropTargetId = isDropTargetTask ? this.dataset.taskId : this.dataset.operationId;\n   561→\n   562→        console.log(`[DRAG] Valid drop: Moving ${isDraggedTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${draggedId} near ${isDropTargetTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${dropTargetId}`);\n   563→\n   564→        // Get the bounding rectangle of the drop target\n   565→        const rect = this.getBoundingClientRect();\n   566→        const midpoint = rect.top + rect.height / 2;\n   567→\n   568→        // Insert before or after based on mouse position\n   569→        const insertBefore = e.clientY < midpoint;\n   570→        console.log(`[DRAG] Insert position: ${insertBefore ? 'before' : 'after'} drop target`);\n   571→\n   572→        if (insertBefore) {\n   573→            this.parentNode.insertBefore(draggedElement, this);\n   574→        } else {\n   575→            this.parentNode.insertBefore(draggedElement, this.nextSibling);\n   576→        }\n   577→\n   578→        console.log('[DRAG] Element moved in DOM, calling saveOrder()');\n   579→        // Save new order\n   580→        saveOrder(draggedElement);\n   581→    } else {\n   582→        if (draggedElement === this) {\n   583→            console.log('[DRAG] Drop ignored: Element dropped on itself');\n   584→        } else if (!isSameType) {\n   585→            console.log('[DRAG] Drop ignored: Different element types (task vs operation)');\n   586→        }\n   587→    }\n   588→\n   589→    return false;\n   590→}\n   591→\n   592→function handleDragEnd(e) {\n   593→    this.classList.remove('dragging');\n   594→\n   595→    // Console tracing for drag end\n   596→    const isTask = this.classList.contains('task-item');\n   597→    const id = isTask ? this.dataset.taskId : this.dataset.operationId;\n   598→    console.log(`[DRAG] End: ${isTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${id}`);\n   599→}\n   600→\n   601→/**\n   602→ * Save new order after drag and drop\n   603→ * Only saves the dragged element's new order position.\n   604→ * The backend will recalculate the order for all other elements.\n   605→ */\n   606→function saveOrder(element) {\n   607→    console.log('[SAVE_ORDER] Function called');\n   608→\n   609→    const isTask = element.classList.contains('task-item');\n   610→    const elementId = isTask ? element.dataset.taskId : element.dataset.operationId;\n   611→    console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Element type: ${isTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'}, ID: ${elementId}`);\n   612→\n   613→    // Get all siblings of the same type to calculate the new order position\n   614→    const siblings = Array.from(element.parentNode.children).filter(el =>\n   615→        el.classList.contains(isTask ? 'task-item' : 'operation-item')\n   616→    );\n   617→\n   618→    console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Found ${siblings.length} siblings of the same type`);\n   619→\n   620→    // Calculate the new order for the dragged element only\n   621→    const newOrder = siblings.indexOf(element) + 1;\n   622→    console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Dragged element new order: ${newOrder}`);\n   623→\n   624→    // Update the data-order attribute immediately for UI consistency\n   625→    element.dataset.order = newOrder;\n   626→\n   627→    // Send update to server only for the dragged element\n   628→    const formData = new FormData();\n   629→    formData.append('_xsrf', xsrf);\n   630→\n   631→    const url = `https://${window.location.host}/${db}/_m_ord/${elementId}?JSON&order=${newOrder}`;\n   632→    console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Sending API request for ${isTask ? 'task' : 'operation'} ${elementId}: ${url}`);\n   633→\n   634→    fetch(url, {\n   635→        method: 'POST',\n   636→        body: formData\n   637→    })\n   638→    .then(response => {\n   639→        console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] API response for ${isTask ? 'task' : 'operation'} ${elementId}: Status ${response.status}`);\n   640→        return response.json();\n   641→    })\n   642→    .then(data => {\n   643→        console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Order updated for ${isTask ? 'task' : 'operation'} ${elementId}: ${newOrder}`, data);\n   644→        // Reload to show updated order from server (backend recalculates all orders)\n   645→        if (selectedProject) {\n   646→            console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Reloading project details for project ${selectedProject['ПроектID']}`);\n   647→            loadProjectDetails(selectedProject['ПроектID']);\n   648→        }\n   649→    })\n   650→    .catch(error => {\n   651→        console.error(`[SAVE_ORDER] Error updating order for ${isTask ? 'task' : 'operation'} ${elementId}:`, error);\n   652→        alert('Ошибка сохранения порядка');\n   653→        // Reload anyway to restore correct state\n   654→        if (selectedProject) {\n   655→            console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Reloading project details after error for project ${selectedProject['ПроектID']}`);\n   656→            loadProjectDetails(selectedProject['ПроектID']);\n   657→        }\n   658→    });\n   659→}\n   660→\n   661→/**\n   662→ * Show add project modal\n   663→ */\n   664→function showAddProjectModal() {\n   665→    document.getElementById('projectModalTitle').textContent = 'Добавить проект';\n   666→    document.getElementById('projectForm').reset();\n   667→    document.getElementById('projectId').value = '';\n   668→    document.getElementById('projectModalBackdrop').classList.add('show');\n   669→}\n   670→\n   671→/**\n   672→ * Close project modal\n   673→ */\n   674→function closeProjectModal() {\n   675→    document.getElementById('projectModalBackdrop').classList.remove('show');\n   676→}\n   677→\n   678→/**\n   679→ * Edit project\n   680→ */\n   681→function editProject() {\n   682→    if (!selectedProject) return;\n   683→\n   684→    document.getElementById('projectModalTitle').textContent = 'Редактировать проект';\n   685→    document.getElementById('projectId').value = the project list data\n   688→\n   689→    // Set client if available\n   690→    const clientSelect = document.getElementById('projectClient');\n   691→    const clientOption = Array.from(clientSelect.options).find(opt =>\n   692→        opt.textContent === selectedProject['Заказчик']\n   693→    );\n   694→    if (clientOption) {\n   695→        clientSelect.value = clientOption.value;\n   696→    }\n   697→\n   698→    // Set status if available\n   699→    const statusSelect = document.getElementById('projectStatus');\n   700→    const statusOption = Array.from(statusSelect.options).find(opt =>\n   701→        opt.textContent === selectedProject['Статус проекта']\n   702→    );\n   703→    if (statusOption) {\n   704→        statusSelect.value = statusOption.value;\n   705→    }\n   706→\n   707→    // Set object if available\n   708→    const objectSelect = document.getElementById('projectObject');\n   709→    const objectOption = Array.from(objectSelect.options).find(opt =>\n   710→        opt.textContent === selectedProject['Объект']\n   711→    );\n   712→    if (objectOption) {\n   713→        objectSelect.value = add task modal\n   729→ */\n   730→function showAddTaskModal() {\n   731→    if (!selectedProject) return;\n   732→\n   733→    document.getElementById('taskModalTitle').textContent = 'Добавить closeTaskModal() {\n   744→    document.getElementById('taskModalBackdrop').classList.remove('show');\n   745→}\n   746→\n   747→/**\n   748→ * Edit task\n   749→ */\n   750→function editTask(taskId) document.getElementById('taskModalTitle').textContent = 'Редактировать задачу';\n   755→    document.getElementById('taskId').value = taskId;\n   756→    document.getElementById('taskProjectId').value =>\n   763→        opt.textContent === taskData['Статус задачи']\n   764→    );\n   765→    if (statusOption) {\n   766→        statusSelect.value = statusOption.value;\n   767→    }\n   768→\n   769→    // Set quantity and unit\n   770→    document.getElementById('taskQuantity').value = taskData['К-во'] || '';\n   771→    const unitSelect = document.getElementById('taskUnit');\n   772→    const */\n   785→function showAddOperationModal(taskId) {\n   786→    document.getElementById('operationModalTitle').textContent = 'Добавить операцию';\n   787→ 804→/**\n   805→ * Edit operation\n   806→ */\n   807→function editOperation(operationId) {\n   808→    const opData = projectDetails.find(item => item['ОперацияID'] === operationId);\n   809→    if (!opData) return;\n   810→\n   811→    document.getElementById('operationModalTitle').textContent = 'Редактировать операцию';\n   812→    document.getElementById('operationId').value = operationId;\n   813→    document.getElementById('operationTaskId').value = opData['Задача проектаID'];\n   814→\n   815→    // Find the operation template in dictionaries\n   816→    const template = dictionaries.operationTemplates.find(t =>\n   817→        t['Операция (шаблон)'] === opData['Операция']\n   818→    );\n   819→\n   820→    // Reset filters first\n   821→    resetOperationFilters();\n   822→\n   823→    // If template has direction and work type, set filters accordingly\n   824→    if (template) {\n   825→        const direction = template['Направление'];\n   826→        const workType = template['Вид работ'];\n   827→\n   828→        // Set direction and trigger change\n   829→        if (direction) {\n   830→            const directionSelect = document.getElementById('operationDirection');\n   831→            if (directionSelect) {\n   832→                directionSelect.value = direction;\n   833→                // Manually trigger the change event to populate work types\n   834→                onDirectionChange({ target: directionSelect });\n   835→\n   836→                // Set work type if available\n   837→                if (workType) {\n   838→                    setTimeout(() => {\n   839→                        const workTypeSelect = document.getElementById('operationWorkType');\n   840→                        if (workTypeSelect) {\n   841→                            workTypeSelect.value = workType;\n   842→                            // Trigger change to filter operations\n   843→                            onWorkTypeChange({ target: workTypeSelect });\n   844→                        }\n   845→                    }, 0);\n   846→                }\n   847→            }\n   848→        }\n   849→    } else {\n   850→        // If no direction/work type, show all operations\n   851→        populateSelect('operationTemplate', dictionaries.operationTemplates, 'Операция (шаблон)', 'Операция (шаблон)ID');\n   852→    }\n   853→\n   854→    // Set operation template after filters are applied\n   855→    setTimeout(() => {\n   856→        const templateSelect = document.getElementById('operationTemplate');\n   857→        const templateOption = Array.from(templateSelect.options).find(opt =>\n   858→            opt.textContent === opData['Операция']\n   859→        );\n   860→        if (templateOption) {\n   861→            templateSelect.value = templateOption.value;\n   862→        }\n   863→    }, 100);\n   864→\n   865→    document.getElementById('operationNorm').value = ''; // Not in response\n   866→    document.getElementById('operationQuantity').value = opData['Операция Кол-во'] || '';\n   867→\n   868→    // Set unit\n   869→    const unitSelect = document.getElementById('operationUnit');\n   870→    const unitOption = Array.from(unitSelect.options).find(opt =>\n   871→        opt.textContent === opData['Операция Ед.изм.']\n   872→    );\n   873→    if (unitOption) {\n   874→        unitSelect.value = unitOption.value;\n   875→    }\n   876→\n   877→    // Set start time\n   878→    if (opData['Операция Начать']) {\n   879→        document.getElementById('operationStart').value = formatDateTimeForInput(opData['Операция Начать']);\n   880→    }\n   881→\n   882→    document.getElementById('operationModalBackdrop').classList.add('show');\n   883→}\n   884→\n   885→/**\n   886→ * Handle project form submission\n   887→ */\n   888→document.getElementById('projectForm').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {\n   889→    e.preventDefault();\n   890→\n   891→    const projectId = document.getElementById('projectId').value;\n   892→    const formData = new FormData();\n   893→    formData.append('_xsrf', xsrf);\n   894→    formData.append('t663', document.getElementById('projectName').value);\n   895→    formData.append('t664', document.getElementById('projectDescription').value);\n   896→    formData.append('t667', document.getElementById('projectClient').value);\n   897→    formData.append('t670', document.getElementById('projectStatus').value);\n   898→    formData.append('t717', document.getElementById('projectObject').value);\n   899→    formData.append('t672', document.getElementById('projectStart').value);\n   900→    formData.append('t674', document.getElementById('projectDeadline').value);\n   901→    formData.append('t677', document.getElementById('projectBudget').value);\n   902→\n   903→    const url = projectId ?\n   904→        `https://${window.location.host}/${db}/_m_new/663?JSON&up=1&id=${projectId}` :\n   905→        `https://${window.location.host}/${db}/_m_new/663?JSON&up=1`;\n   906→\n   907→    fetch(url, {\n   908→        method: 'POST',\n   909→        body: formData\n   910→    })\n   911→    .then(response => response.json())\n   912→    .then(data => {\n   913→        console.log('Project saved:', data);\n   914→        closeProjectModal();\n   915→        loadProjects();\n   916→    })\n   917→    .catch(error => {\n   918→        console.error('Error saving project:', error);\n   919→        alert('Ошибка сохранения проекта');\n   920→    });\n   921→});\n   922→\n   923→/**\n   924→ * Handle task form submission\n   925→ */\n   926→document.getElementById('taskForm').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {\n   927→    e.preventDefault();\n   928→\n   929→    const taskId = document.getElementById('taskId').value;\n   930→    const projectId = document.getElementById('taskProjectId').value;\n   931→    const formData = new FormData();\n   932→    formData.append('_xsrf', 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${id}, Order=${this.dataset.order}`);\n}\n\nfunction handleDragOver(e) {\n    if (e.preventDefault) {\n        e.preventDefault();\n    }\n    e.dataTransfer.dropEffect = 'move';\n\n    // Console tracing for drag over (throttled to avoid spam)\n    if (!this._lastDragOverLog || Date.now() - this._lastDragOverLog > 500) {\n        const isTask = this.classList.contains('task-item');\n        const id = isTask ? this.dataset.taskId : this.dataset.operationId;\n        console.log(`[DRAG] Over: ${isTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${id}`);\n        this._lastDragOverLog = Date.now();\n    }\n\n    return false;\n}\n\nfunction handleDrop(e) {\n    if (e.stopPropagation) {\n        e.stopPropagation();\n    }\n\n    console.log('[DRAG] Drop event triggered');\n\n    // Check if both elements are of the same type (both tasks or both operations)\n    const isDraggedTask = draggedElement.classList.contains('task-item');\n    const isDraggedOperation = draggedElement.classList.contains('operation-item');\n    const isDropTargetTask = this.classList.contains('task-item');\n    const isDropTargetOperation = this.classList.contains('operation-item');\n    const isSameType = (isDraggedTask && isDropTargetTask) || (isDraggedOperation && isDropTargetOperation);\n\n    if (draggedElement !== this && isSameType) {\n        const draggedId = isDraggedTask ? draggedElement.dataset.taskId : draggedElement.dataset.operationId;\n        const dropTargetId = isDropTargetTask ? this.dataset.taskId : this.dataset.operationId;\n\n        console.log(`[DRAG] Valid drop: Moving ${isDraggedTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${draggedId} near ${isDropTargetTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${dropTargetId}`);\n\n        // Get the bounding rectangle of the drop target\n        const rect = this.getBoundingClientRect();\n        const midpoint = rect.top + rect.height / 2;\n\n        // Insert before or after based on mouse position\n        const insertBefore = e.clientY < midpoint;\n        console.log(`[DRAG] Insert position: ${insertBefore ? 'before' : 'after'} drop target`);\n\n        if (insertBefore) {\n            this.parentNode.insertBefore(draggedElement, this);\n        } else {\n            this.parentNode.insertBefore(draggedElement, this.nextSibling);\n        }\n\n        console.log('[DRAG] Element moved in DOM, calling saveOrder()');\n        // Save new order\n        saveOrder(draggedElement);\n    } else {\n        if (draggedElement === this) {\n            console.log('[DRAG] Drop ignored: Element dropped on itself');\n        } else if (!isSameType) {\n            console.log('[DRAG] Drop ignored: Different element types (task vs operation)');\n        }\n    }\n\n    return false;\n}\n\nfunction handleDragEnd(e) {\n    this.classList.remove('dragging');\n\n    // Console tracing for drag end\n    const isTask = this.classList.contains('task-item');\n    const id = isTask ? this.dataset.taskId : this.dataset.operationId;\n    console.log(`[DRAG] End: ${isTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${id}`);\n}\n\n/**\n * Save new order after drag and drop\n * Only saves the dragged element's new order position.\n * The backend will recalculate the order for all other elements.\n */\nfunction saveOrder(element) {\n    console.log('[SAVE_ORDER] Function called');\n\n    const isTask = element.classList.contains('task-item');\n    const elementId = isTask ? element.dataset.taskId : element.dataset.operationId;\n    console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Element type: ${isTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'}, ID: ${elementId}`);\n\n    // Get all siblings of the same type to calculate the new order position\n    const siblings = Array.from(element.parentNode.children).filter(el =>\n        el.classList.contains(isTask ? 'task-item' : 'operation-item')\n    );\n\n    console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Found ${siblings.length} siblings of the same type`);\n\n    // Calculate the new order for the dragged element only\n    const newOrder = siblings.indexOf(element) + 1;\n    console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Dragged element new order: ${newOrder}`);\n\n    // Update the data-order attribute immediately for UI consistency\n    element.dataset.order = newOrder;\n\n    // Send update to server only for the dragged element\n    const formData = new FormData();\n    formData.append('_xsrf', xsrf);\n\n    const url = `https://${window.location.host}/${db}/_m_ord/${elementId}?JSON&order=${newOrder}`;\n    console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Sending API request for ${isTask ? 'task' : 'operation'} ${elementId}: ${url}`);\n\n    fetch(url, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        body: formData\n    })\n    .then(response => {\n        console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] API response for ${isTask ? 'task' : 'operation'} ${elementId}: Status ${response.status}`);\n        return response.json();\n    })\n    .then(data => {\n        console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Order updated for ${isTask ? 'task' : 'operation'} ${elementId}: ${newOrder}`, data);\n        // Reload to show updated order from server (backend recalculates all orders)\n        if (selectedProject) {\n            console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Reloading project details for project ${selectedProject['ПроектID']}`);\n            loadProjectDetails(selectedProject['ПроектID']);\n        }\n    })\n    .catch(error => {\n        console.error(`[SAVE_ORDER] Error updating order for ${isTask ? 'task' : 'operation'} ${elementId}:`, error);\n        alert('Ошибка сохранения порядка');\n        // Reload anyway to restore correct state\n        if (selectedProject) {\n            console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Reloading project details after error for project ${selectedP
[2025-12-27T15:40:25.946Z] [INFO] roject['ПроектID']}`);\n            loadProjectDetails(selectedProject['ПроектID']);\n        }\n    });\n}\n\n/**\n * Show add project modal\n */\nfunction          task: item,\n                operations: []\n            };\n        }\n        if (item['ОперацияID']) {\n            taskGroups[taskId].operations.push(item);\n        }\n    });\n\n    // 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${id}, Order=${this.dataset.order}`);\n}\n\nfunction handleDragOver(e) {\n    if (e.preventDefault) {\n        e.preventDefault();\n    }\n    e.dataTransfer.dropEffect = 'move';\n\n    // Console tracing for drag over (throttled to avoid spam)\n    if (!this._lastDragOverLog || Date.now() - this._lastDragOverLog > 500) {\n        const isTask = this.classList.contains('task-item');\n        const id = isTask ? this.dataset.taskId : this.dataset.operationId;\n        console.log(`[DRAG] Over: ${isTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${id}`);\n        this._lastDragOverLog = Date.now();\n    }\n\n    return false;\n}\n\nfunction handleDrop(e) {\n    if (e.stopPropagation) {\n        e.stopPropagation();\n    }\n\n    console.log('[DRAG] Drop event triggered');\n\n    // Check if both elements are of the same type (both tasks or both operations)\n    const isDraggedTask = draggedElement.classList.contains('task-item');\n    const isDraggedOperation = draggedElement.classList.contains('operation-item');\n    const isDropTargetTask = this.classList.contains('task-item');\n    const isDropTargetOperation = this.classList.contains('operation-item');\n    const isSameType = (isDraggedTask && isDropTargetTask) || (isDraggedOperation && isDropTargetOperation);\n\n    if (draggedElement !== this && isSameType) {\n        const draggedId = isDraggedTask ? draggedElement.dataset.taskId : draggedElement.dataset.operationId;\n        const dropTargetId = isDropTargetTask ? this.dataset.taskId : this.dataset.operationId;\n\n        console.log(`[DRAG] Valid drop: Moving ${isDraggedTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${draggedId} near ${isDropTargetTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${dropTargetId}`);\n\n        // Get the bounding rectangle of the drop target\n        const rect = this.getBoundingClientRect();\n        const midpoint = rect.top + rect.height / 2;\n\n        // Insert before or after based on mouse position\n        const insertBefore = e.clientY < midpoint;\n        console.log(`[DRAG] Insert position: ${insertBefore ? 'before' : 'after'} drop target`);\n\n        if (insertBefore) {\n            this.parentNode.insertBefore(draggedElement, this);\n        } else {\n            this.parentNode.insertBefore(draggedElement, this.nextSibling);\n        }\n\n        console.log('[DRAG] Element moved in DOM, calling saveOrder()');\n        // Save new order\n        saveOrder(draggedElement);\n    } else {\n        if (draggedElement === this) {\n            console.log('[DRAG] Drop ignored: Element dropped on itself');\n        } else if (!isSameType) {\n            console.log('[DRAG] Drop ignored: Different element types (task vs operation)');\n        }\n    }\n\n    return false;\n}\n\nfunction handleDragEnd(e) {\n    this.classList.remove('dragging');\n\n    // Console tracing for drag end\n    const isTask = this.classList.contains('task-item');\n    const id = isTask ? this.dataset.taskId : this.dataset.operationId;\n    console.log(`[DRAG] End: ${isTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${id}`);\n}\n\n/**\n * Save new order after drag and drop\n * Only saves the dragged element's new order position.\n * The backend will recalculate the order for all other elements.\n */\nfunction saveOrder(element) {\n    console.log('[SAVE_ORDER] Function called');\n\n    const isTask = element.classList.contains('task-item');\n    const elementId = isTask ? element.dataset.taskId : element.dataset.operationId;\n    console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Element type: ${isTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'}, ID: ${elementId}`);\n\n    // Get all siblings of the same type to calculate the new order position\n    const siblings = Array.from(element.parentNode.children).filter(el =>\n        el.classList.contains(isTask ? 'task-item' : 'operation-item')\n    );\n\n    console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Found ${siblings.length} siblings of the same type`);\n\n    // Calculate the new order for the dragged element only\n    const newOrder = siblings.indexOf(element) + 1;\n    console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Dragged element new order: ${newOrder}`);\n\n    // Update the data-order attribute immediately for UI consistency\n    element.dataset.order = newOrder;\n\n    // Send update to server only for the dragged element\n    const formData = new FormData();\n    formData.append('_xsrf', xsrf);\n\n    const url = `https://${window.location.host}/${db}/_m_ord/${elementId}?JSON&order=${newOrder}`;\n    console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Sending API request for ${isTask ? 'task' : 'operation'} ${elementId}: ${url}`);\n\n    fetch(url, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        body: formData\n    })\n    .then(response => {\n        console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] API response for ${isTask ? 'task' : 'operation'} ${elementId}: Status ${response.status}`);\n        return response.json();\n    })\n    .then(data => {\n        console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Order updated for ${isTask ? 'task' : 'operation'} ${elementId}: ${newOrder}`, data);\n        // Reload to show updated order from server (backend recalculates all orders)\n        if (selectedProject) {\n            console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Reloading project details for project ${selectedProject['ПроектID']}`);\n            loadProjectDetails(selectedProject['ПроектID']);\n        }\n    })\n    .catch(error => {\n        console.error(`[SAVE_ORDER] Error updating order for ${isTask ? 'task' : 'operation'} ${elementId}:`, error);\n        alert('Ошибка сохранения порядка');\n        // Reload anyway to restore correct state\n        if (selectedProject) {\n            console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Reloading project details after error for project ${selectedProject['ПроектID']}`);\n            loadProjectDetails(selectedProject['ПроектID']);\n        }\n    });\n}\n\n/**\n * Show add project modal\n */\nfunction showAddProjectModal() {\n    document.getElementById('projectModalTitle').textContent = 'Добавить проект';\n '<br><small>Статус: ' + escapeHtml(task['Статус задачи']) + '</small>' : ''}\n                </div>\n                <div class=\"task-actions\">\n                    <button class=\"btn btn-sm btn-primary\" onclick=\"showAddOperationModal('${taskId}')\">+ Операция</button>\n                    <button class=\"btn btn-sm btn-secondary\" onclick=\"editTask('${taskId}')\">Изм.</button>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        `;\n\n        // Add operations\n        operations.forEach((op, opIndex) => {\n            if (op['ОперацияID']) {\n                html += `\n                    <div class=\"operation-item\" draggable=\"true\" data-operation-id=\"${op['ОперацияID']}\" data-order=\"${op['ОперацияOrder']}\">\n                        <span class=\"drag-handle\">☰</span>\n                        <span class=\"operation-order\">${opIndex + 1}</span>\n                        <div class=\"operation-content\">\n                            ${escapeHtml(op['Операция'] || 'Без названия')}\n                            ${op['Операция Начать'] ? '<br><small>Начать: ' + escapeHtml(op['Операция Начать']) + '</small>' : ''}\n                            ${op['Операция Кол-во'] ? '<br><small>Кол-во: ' + escapeHtml(op['Операция Кол-во']) + ' ' + escapeHtml(op['Операция Ед.изм.'] || '') + '</small>' : ''}\n                        </div>\n                        <div class=\"operation-actions\">\n                            <button class=\"btn btn-sm btn-secondary\" onclick=\"editOperation('${op['ОперацияID']}')\">Изм.</button>\n                        </div>\n                    </div>\n                `;\n            }\n        });\n\n        return html;\n    }).join('');\n\n    // Add drag and drop handlers\n    addDragAndDropHandlers();\n}\n\n/**\n * Add drag and drop handlers for reordering\n */\nfunction addDragAndDropHandlers() {\n    const tasks = document.querySelectorAll('.task-item');\n    const operations = document.querySelectorAll('.operation-item');\n\n    tasks.forEach(task => {\n        task.addEventListener('dragstart', handleDragStart);\n        task.addEventListener('dragover', handleDragOver);\n        task.addEventListener('drop', handleDrop);\n        task.addEventListener('dragend', handleDragEnd);\n    });\n\n    operations.forEach(operation => {\n        operation.addEventListener('dragstart', handleDragStart);\n        operation.addEventListener('dragover', handleDragOver);\n        operation.addEventListener('drop', handleDrop);\n        operation.addEventListener('dragend', handleDragEnd);\n    });\n}\n\nlet draggedElement = null;\n\nfunction handleDragStart(e) {\n    draggedElement = this;\n    this.classList.add('dragging');\n    e.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'move';\n\n    // Console tracing for drag start\n    const isTask = this.classList.contains('task-item');\n    const id = isTask ? this.dataset.taskId : this.dataset.operationId;\n    console.log(`[DRAG] Start: ${isTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${id}, Order=${this.dataset.order}`);\n}\n\nfunction handleDragOver(e) {\n    if (e.preventDefault) {\n        e.preventDefault();\n    }\n    e.dataTransfer.dropEffect = 'move';\n\n    // Console tracing for drag over (throttled to avoid spam)\n    if (!this._lastDragOverLog || Date.now() - this._lastDragOverLog > 500) {\n        const isTask = this.classList.contains('task-item');\n        const id = isTask ? this.dataset.taskId : this.dataset.operationId;\n        console.log(`[DRAG] Over: ${isTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${id}`);\n        this._lastDragOverLog = Date.now();\n    }\n\n    return false;\n}\n\nfunction handleDrop(e) {\n    if (e.stopPropagation) {\n        e.stopPropagation();\n    }\n\n    console.log('[DRAG] Drop event triggered');\n\n    // Check if both elements are of the same type (both tasks or both operations)\n    const isDraggedTask = draggedElement.classList.contains('task-item');\n    const isDraggedOperation = draggedElement.classList.contains('operation-item');\n    const isDropTargetTask = this.classList.contains('task-item');\n    const isDropTargetOperation = this.classList.contains('operation-item');\n    const isSameType = (isDraggedTask && isDropTargetTask) || (isDraggedOperation && isDropTargetOperation);\n\n    if (draggedElement !== this && isSameType) {\n        const draggedId = isDraggedTask ? draggedElement.dataset.taskId : draggedElement.dataset.operationId;\n        const dropTargetId = isDropTargetTask ? this.dataset.taskId : this.dataset.operationId;\n\n        console.log(`[DRAG] Valid drop: Moving ${isDraggedTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${draggedId} near ${isDropTargetTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${dropTargetId}`);\n\n        // Get the bounding rectangle of the drop target\n        const rect = this.getBoundingClientRect();\n        const midpoint = rect.top + rect.height / 2;\n\n        // Insert before or after based on mouse position\n        const insertBefore = e.clientY < midpoint;\n        console.log(`[DRAG] Insert position: ${insertBefore ? 'before' : 'after'} drop target`);\n\n        if (insertBefore) {\n            this.parentNode.insertBefore(draggedElement, this);\n        } else {\n            this.parentNode.insertBefore(draggedElement, this.nextSibling);\n        }\n\n        console.log('[DRAG] Element moved in DOM, calling saveOrder()');\n        // Save new order\n        saveOrder(draggedElement);\n    } else {\n        if (draggedElement === this) {\n            console.log('[DRAG] Drop ignored: Element dropped on itself');\n        } else if (!isSameType) {\n            console.log('[DRAG] Drop ignored: Different element types (task vs operation)');\n        }\n    }\n\n    return false;\n}\n\nfunction handleDragEnd(e) {\n    this.classList.remove('dragging');\n\n    // Console tracing for drag end\n    const isTask = this.classList.contains('task-item');\n    const id = isTask ? this.dataset.taskId : this.dataset.operationId;\n    console.log(`[DRAG] End: ${isTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${id}`);\n}\n\n/**\n * Save new order after drag and drop\n * Only saves the dragged element's new order position.\n * The backend will recalculate the order for all other elements.\n */\nfunction saveOrder(element) {\n    console.log('[SAVE_ORDER] Function called');\n\n    const isTask = element.classList.contains('task-item');\n    const elementId = isTask ? element.dataset.taskId : element.dataset.operationId;\n    console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Element type: ${isTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'}, ID: ${elementId}`);\n\n    // Get all siblings of the same type to calculate the new order position\n    const siblings = Array.from(element.parentNode.children).filter(el =>\n        el.classList.contains(isTask ? 'task-item' : 'operation-item')\n    );\n\n    console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Found ${siblings.length} siblings of the same type`);\n\n    // Calculate the new order for the dragged element only\n    const newOrder = siblings.indexOf(element) + 1;\n    console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Dragged element new order: ${newOrder}`);\n\n    // Update the data-order attribute immediately for UI consistency\n    element.dataset.order = newOrder;\n\n    // Send update to server only for the dragged element\n    const formData = new FormData();\n    formData.append('_xsrf', xsrf);\n\n    const url = `https://${window.location.host}/${db}/_m_ord/${elementId}?JSON&order=${newOrder}`;\n    console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Sending API request for ${isTask ? 'task' : 'operation'} ${elementId}: ${url}`);\n\n    fetch(url, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        body: formData\n    })\n    .then(response => {\n        console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] API response for ${isTask ? 'task' : 'operation'} ${elementId}: Status ${response.status}`);\n        return response.json();\n    })\n    .then(data => {\n        console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Order updated for ${isTask ? 'task' : 'operation'} ${elementId}: ${newOrder}`, data);\n        // Reload to show updated order from server (backend recalculates all orders)\n        if (selectedProject) {\n            console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Reloading project details for project ${selectedProject['ПроектID']}`);\n            loadProjectDetails(selectedProject['ПроектID']);\n        }\n    })\n    .catch(error => {\n        console.error(`[SAVE_ORDER] Error updating order for ${isTask ? 'task' : 'operation'} ${elementId}:`, error);\n        alert('Ошибка сохранения порядка');\n        // Reload anyway to restore correct state\n        if (selectedProject) {\n            console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Reloading project details after error for project ${selectedProject['ПроектID']}`);\n            loadProjectDetails(selectedProject['ПроектID']);\n        }\n    });\n}\n\n/**\n * Show add project modal\n */\nfunction showAddProjectModal() {\n    document.getElementById('projectModalTitle').textContent = 'Добавить проект';\n     .then(data => {\n            dictionaries.operationTemplates = data;\n\n            // Extract unique directions and work types\n            extractDirectionsAndWorkTypes(data);\n\n            // Populate direction dropdown\n            populateDirectionSelect();\n\n            // Don't populate operation template dropdown initially - wait for filters\n            // populateSelect('operationTemplate', data, 'Операция (шаблон)', 'Операция (шаблон)ID');\n        })\n        .catch(error => console.error('Error loading operation templates:', error));\n\n    // Load project statuses (Статусы проекта)\n    fetch(`https://${window.location.host}/${db}/report/6052?JSON_KV`)\n        .then(response => response.json())\n        .then(data => {\n            dictionaries.projectStatuses = data;\n            populateSelect('projectStatus', data, 'Статус проекта', 'Статус проектаID');\n        })\n        .catch(error => console.error('Error loading project statuses:', error));\n\n    // Load task statuses (Статусы задачи)\n    fetch(`https://${window.location.host}/${db}/report/6058?JSON_KV`)\n        .then(response => response.json())\n        .then(data => {\n            dictionaries.taskStatuses = data;\n            populateSelect('taskStatus', data, 'Статус задачи', 'Статус задачиID');\n        })\n        .catch(error => console.error('Error loading task statuses:', error));\n\n    // Load metadata to get clients and objects\n    fetch(`https://${window.location.host}/${db}/metadata`)\n        .then(response => response.json())\n        .then(metadata => {\n            // Find clients table (id 665)\n            const clientsTable = metadata.find(t => t.id === '665');\n            if (clientsTable) {\n                loadTableData(665, 'clients', 'Заказчик', 'ЗаказчикID');\n            }\n\n            // Find objects table (id 715)\n            const objectsTable = metadata.find(t => t.id === '715');\n            if (objectsTable) {\n                loadTableData(715, 'objects', 'Объект ', 'Объект ID');\n            }\n        })\n        .catch(error => console.error('Error loading metadata:', error));\n}\n\n/**\n * Load table data for dictionaries\n */\nfunction loadTableData(tableId, dictKey, labelField, idField) {\n    fetch(`https://${window.location.host}/${db}/report/22?JSON_KV&FR_table=${tableId}`)\n        .then(response => response.json())\n        .then(data => {\n            dictionaries[dictKey] = data;\n            const selectId = dictKey === 'clients' ? 'projectClient' : 'projectObject';\n            populateSelect(selectId, data, labelField, idField);\n        })\n        .catch(error => console.error(`Error loading ${dictKey}:`, error));\n}\n\n/**\n * Populate a select element with options\n */\nfunction populateSelect(selectId, data, labelField, idField) {\n    const select = document.getElementById(selectId);\n    if (!select) return;\n\n    // Clear existing options except the first one\n    while (select.options.length > 1) {\n        select.remove(1);\n    }\n\n    // Add new options\n    data.forEach(item => {\n        const option = document.createElement('option');\n        option.value = item[idField];\n        option.textContent = item[labelField];\n        select.appendChild(option);\n    });\n}\n\n/**\n * Extract unique directions and work types from operation templates\n */\nfunction extractDirectionsAndWorkTypes(templates) {\n    const directionsSet = new Set();\n    const workTypesMap = new Map(); // Map direction to work types\n\n    templates.forEach(template => {\n        const direction = template['Направление'];\n        const workType = template['Вид работ'];\n\n        if (direction) {\n            directionsSet.add(direction);\n\n            if (workType) {\n                if (!workTypesMap.has(direction)) {\n                    workTypesMap.set(direction, new Set());\n                }\n                workTypesMap.get(direction).add(workType);\n            }\n        }\n    });\n\n    // Convert sets to arrays\n    dictionaries.directions = Array.from(directionsSet).map(name => ({ name }));\n    dictionaries.workTypesMap = workTypesMap;\n}\n\n/**\n * Populate direction select dropdown\n */\nfunction populateDirectionSelect() {\n    const select = document.getElementById('operationDirection');\n    if (!select) return;\n\n    // Clear existing options except the first one\n    while (select.options.length > 1) {\n        select.remove(1);\n    }\n\n    // Add new options\n    dictionaries.directions.forEach(direction => {\n        const option = document.createElement('option');\n        option.value = direction.name;\n        option.textContent = direction.name;\n        select.appendChild(option);\n    });\n\n    // Add event listener for direction change\n    select.addEventListener('change', onDirectionChange);\n}\n\n/**\n * Handle direction selection change\n */\nfunction onDirectionChange(event) {\n    const selectedDirection = event.target.value;\n    const workTypeSelect = document.getElementById('operationWorkType');\n    const operationSelect = document.getElementById('operationTemplate');\n\n    // Reset work type dropdown\n    if (workTypeSelect) {\n        while (workTypeSelect.options.length > 1) {\n            workTypeSelect.remove(1);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Reset operation template dropdown\n    if (operationSelect) {\n        while (operationSelect.options.length > 1) {\n            operationSelect.remove(1);\n        }\n    }\n\n    if (!selectedDirection) {\n        return;\n    }\n\n    // Populate work types for selected direction\n    const workTypes = dictionaries.workTypesMap.get(selectedDirection);\n    if (workTypes && workTypeSelect) {\n        Array.from(workTypes).forEach(workType => {\n            const option = document.createElement('option');\n            option.value = workType;\n            option.textContent = workType;\n            workTypeSelect.appendChild(option);\n        });\n\n        // Add event listener for work type change\n        workTypeSelect.removeEventListener('change', onWorkTypeChange);\n        workTypeSelect.addEventListener('change', onWorkTypeChange);\n    }\n\n    // If no work types exist for this direction, filter operations directly\n    if (!workTypes || workTypes.size === 0) {\n        filterOperationTemplates(selectedDirection, null);\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Handle work type selection change\n */\nfunction onWorkTypeChange(event) {\n    const selectedDirection = document.getElementById('operationDirection').value;\n    const selectedWorkType = event.target.value;\n\n    filterOperationTemplates(selectedDirection, selectedWorkType);\n}\n\n/**\n * Filter operation templates based on direction and work type\n */\nfunction filterOperationTemplates(direction, workType) {\n    const operationSelect = document.getElementById('operationTemplate');\n    if (!operationSelect) return;\n\n    // Clear existing options except the first one\n    while (operationSelect.options.length > 1) {\n        operationSelect.remove(1);\n    }\n\n    // Filter templates\n    const filteredTemplates = dictionaries.operationTemplates.filter(template => {\n        const matchesDirection = !direction || template['Направление'] === direction;\n        const matchesWorkType = !workType || template['Вид работ'] === workType;\n        return matchesDirection && matchesWorkType;\n    });\n\n    // Populate filtered options\n    filteredTemplates.forEach(template => {\n        const option = document.createElement('option');\n        option.value = template['Операция (шаблон)ID'];\n        option.textContent = template['Операция (шаблон)'];\n        operationSelect.appendChild(option);\n    });\n}\n\n/**\n * Reset operation filter dropdowns\n */\nfunction resetOperationFilters() {\n    // Reset direction\n    const directionSelect = document.getElementById('operationDirection');\n    if (directionSelect) {\n        directionSelect.value = '';\n    }\n\n    // Reset work type\n    const workTypeSelect = document.getElementById('operationWorkType');\n    if (workTypeSelect) {\n        workTypeSelect.value = '';\n        while (workTypeSelect.options.length > 1) {\n            workTypeSelect.remove(1);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Reset operation template\n    const operationSelect = document.getElementById('operationTemplate');\n    if (operationSelect) {\n        operationSelect.value = '';\n        while (operationSelect.options.length > 1) {\n            operationSelect.remove(1);\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Load all projects\n */\nfunction loadProjects() {\n    fetch(`https://${window.location.host}/${db}/report/4472?JSON_KV`)\n        .then(response => response.json())\n        .then(data => {\n            allProjects = data;\n            displayProjects(data);\n        })\n        .catch(error => {\n            console.error('Error loading projects:', error);\n            alert('Ошибка загрузки проектов');\n        });\n}\n\n/**\n * Display projects in the list\n */\nfunction displayProjects(projects) {\n    const projectList = document.getElementById('projectList');\n    if (!projectList) return;\n\n    if (projects.length === 0) {\n        projectList.innerHTML = '<div style=\"padding: 20px; text-align: center; color: #6c757d;\">Проекты не найдены</div>';\n        return;\n    }\n\n    projectList.innerHTML = projects.map(project => `\n        <div class=\"project-item\" onclick=\"selectProject('${project['ПроектID']}')\" data-project-id=\"${project['ПроектID']}\">\n            <div class=\"project-header\">${escapeHtml(project['Проект'] || 'Без названия')}</div>\n            <div class=\"project-meta\">\n                <span>Заказчик: ${escapeHtml(project['Заказчик'] || '—')}</span> |\n                <span>Старт: ${escapeHtml(project['Старт'] || '—')}</span> |\n                <span>Срок: ${escapeHtml(project['Срок'] || '—')}</span> |\n                <span>Объект: ${escapeHtml(project['Объект'] || '—')}</span> |\n                <span>Статус: ${escapeHtml(project['Статус проекта'] || '—')}</span>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n    `).join('');\n}\n\n/**\n * Filter projects based on search input\n */\nfunction filterProjects() {\n    const searchTerm = document.getElementById('projectSearch').value.toLowerCase();\n\n    const filtered = allProjects.filter(project => {\n        return Object.values(project).some(value =>\n            value && value.toString().toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm)\n        );\n    });\n\n    displayProjects(filtered);\n}\n\n/**\n * Select a project and load its details\n */\nfunction selectProject(projectId) {\n    // Remove active class from all items\n    document.querySelectorAll('.project-item').forEach(item => {\n        item.classList.remove('active');\n    });\n\n    // Add active class to selected item\n    const selectedItem = document.querySelector(`.project-item[data-project-id=\"${projectId}\"]`);\n    if (selectedItem) {\n        selectedItem.classList.add('active');\n    }\n\n    selectedProject = allProjects.find(p => p['ПроектID'] === projectId);\n    if (!selectedProject) return;\n\n    // Update UI\n    document.getElementById('selectedProjectName').textContent = selectedProject['Проект'];\n    document.getElementById('taskSection').classList.add('active');\n\n    // Load project details (tasks and operations)\n    loadProjectDetails(projectId);\n}\n\n/**\n * Load project details (tasks and operations)\n */\nfunction loadProjectDetails(projectId) {\n    fetch(`https://${window.location.host}/${db}/report/5977?JSON_KV&FR_ПроектID=${projectId}`)\n        .then(response => response.json())\n        .then(data => {\n            projectDetails = data;\n            displayTasksAndOperations(data);\n        })\n        .catch(error => {\n            console.error('Error loading project details:', error);\n            alert('Ошибка загрузки задач проекта');\n        });\n}\n\n/**\n * Display tasks and operations\n */\nfunction displayTasksAndOperations(data) {\n    const taskList = document.getElementById('taskList');\n    if (!taskList) return;\n\n    if (data.length === 0) {\n        taskList.innerHTML = '<div style=\"padding: 20px; text-align: center; color: #6c757d;\">Задачи не найдены</div>';\n        return;\n    }\n\n    // Group by tasks\n    const taskGroups = {};\n    data.forEach(item => {\n        const taskId = item['Задача проектаID'];\n        if (!taskGroups[taskId]) {\n            taskGroups[taskId] = {\n                task: item,\n                operations: []\n            };\n        }\n        if (item['ОперацияID']) {\n            taskGroups[taskId].operations.push(item);\n        }\n    });\n\n    // Sort tasks by order\n    const sortedTaskIds = Object.keys(taskGroups).sort((a, b) => {\n        const orderA = parseInt(taskGroups[a].task['Задача проектаOrder'] || 0);\n        const orderB = parseInt(taskGroups[b].task['Задача проектаOrder'] || 0);\n        return orderA - orderB;\n    });\n\n    taskList.innerHTML = sortedTaskIds.map((taskId, index) => {\n        const group = taskGroups[taskId];\n        const task = group.task;\n        const operations = group.operations.sort((a, b) => {\n            const orderA = parseInt(a['ОперацияOrder'] || 0);\n            const orderB = parseInt(b['ОперацияOrder'] || 0);\n            return orderA - orderB;\n        });\n\n        const deleteCheckbox = deleteModeActive ? `<input type=\"checkbox\" class=\"delete-checkbox\" data-type=\"task\" data-id=\"${taskId}\" onchange=\"toggleItemSelection(this)\">` : '';\n        const isSelected = selectedItemsForDeletion.has(`task-${taskId}`) ? 'selected' : '';\n\n        let html = `\n            <div class=\"task-item ${isSelected}\" draggable=\"${!deleteModeActive}\" data-task-id=\"${taskId}\" data-order=\"${task['Задача проектаOrder']}\">\n                ${deleteCheckbox}\n                <span class=\"drag-handle\" style=\"display: ${deleteModeActive ? 'none' : 'inline'}\">☰</span>\n                <span class=\"task-order\">${index + 1}</span>\n                <div class=\"task-content\">\n                    <strong>${escapeHtml(task['Задача проекта'] || 'Без названия')}</strong>\n                    ${task['Задача Описание'] ? '<br><small>' + escapeHtml(task['Задача Описание']) + '</small>' : ''}\n                    ${task['Статус задачи'] ? '<br><small>Статус: ' + escapeHtml(task['Статус задачи']) + '</small>' : ''}\n                </div>\n                <div class=\"task-actions\">\n                    <button class=\"btn btn-sm btn-primary\" onclick=\"showAddOperationModal('${taskId}')\">+ Операция</button>\n                    <button class=\"btn btn-sm btn-secondary\" onclick=\"editTask('${taskId}')\">Изм.</button>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        `;\n\n        // Add operations\n        operations.forEach((op, opIndex) => {\n            if (op['ОперацияID']) {\n                const opDeleteCheckbox = deleteModeActive ? `<input type=\"checkbox\" class=\"delete-checkbox\" data-type=\"operation\" data-id=\"${op['ОперацияID']}\" onchange=\"toggleItemSelection(this)\">` : '';\n                const opIsSelected = selectedItemsForDeletion.has(`operation-${op['ОперацияID']}`) ? 'selected' : '';\n\n                html += `\n                    <div class=\"operation-item ${opIsSelected}\" draggable=\"${!deleteModeActive}\" data-operation-id=\"${op['ОперацияID']}\" data-order=\"${op['ОперацияOrder']}\">\n                        ${opDeleteCheckbox}\n                        <span class=\"drag-handle\" style=\"display: ${deleteModeActive ? 'none' : 'inline'}\">☰</span>\n                        <span class=\"operation-order\">${opIndex + 1}</span>\n                        <div class=\"operation-content\">\n                            ${escapeHtml(op['Операция'] || 'Без названия')}\n                            ${op['Операция Начать'] ? '<br><small>Начать: ' + escapeHtml(op['Операция Начать']) + '</small>' : ''}\n                            ${op['Операция Кол-во'] ? '<br><small>Кол-во: ' + escapeHtml(op['Операция Кол-во']) + ' ' + escapeHtml(op['Операция Ед.изм.'] || '') + '</small>' : ''}\n                        </div>\n                        <div class=\"operation-actions\">\n                            <button class=\"btn btn-sm btn-secondary\" onclick=\"editOperation('${op['ОперацияID']}')\">Изм.</button>\n                        </div>\n                    </div>\n                `;\n            }\n        });\n\n        return html;\n    }).join('');\n\n    // Update delete mode class on task list container\n    if (deleteModeActive) {\n        taskList.classList.add('delete-mode');\n    } else {\n        taskList.classList.remove('delete-mode');\n    }\n\n    // Add drag and drop handlers (only if not in delete mode)\n    if (!deleteModeActive) {\n        addDragAndDropHandlers();\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Add drag and drop handlers for reordering\n */\nfunction addDragAndDropHandlers() {\n    const tasks = document.querySelectorAll('.task-item');\n    const operations = document.querySelectorAll('.operation-item');\n\n    tasks.forEach(task => {\n        task.addEventListener('dragstart', handleDragStart);\n        task.addEventListener('dragover', handleDragOver);\n        task.addEventListener('drop', handleDrop);\n        task.addEventListener('dragend', handleDragEnd);\n    });\n\n    operations.forEach(operation => {\n        operation.addEventListener('dragstart', handleDragStart);\n        operation.addEventListener('dragover', handleDragOver);\n        operation.addEventListener('drop', handleDrop);\n        operation.addEventListener('dragend', handleDragEnd);\n    });\n}\n\nlet draggedElement = null;\n\nfunction handleDragStart(e) {\n    draggedElement = this;\n    this.classList.add('dragging');\n    e.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'move';\n\n    // Console tracing for drag start\n    const isTask = this.classList.contains('task-item');\n    const id = isTask ? this.dataset.taskId : this.dataset.operationId;\n    console.log(`[DRAG] Start: ${isTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${id}, Order=${this.dataset.order}`);\n}\n\nfunction handleDragOver(e) {\n    if (e.preventDefault) {\n        e.preventDefault();\n    }\n    e.dataTransfer.dropEffect = 'move';\n\n    // Console tracing for drag over (throttled to avoid spam)\n    if (!this._lastDragOverLog || Date.now() - this._lastDragOverLog > 500) {\n        const isTask = this.classList.contains('task-item');\n        const id = isTask ? this.dataset.taskId : this.dataset.operationId;\n        console.log(`[DRAG] Over: ${isTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${id}`);\n        this._lastDragOverLog = Date.now();\n    }\n\n    return false;\n}\n\nfunction handleDrop(e) {\n    if (e.stopPropagation) {\n        e.stopPropagation();\n    }\n\n    console.log('[DRAG] Drop event triggered');\n\n    // Check if both elements are of the same type (both tasks or both operations)\n    const isDraggedTask = draggedElement.classList.contains('task-item');\n    const isDraggedOperation = draggedElement.classList.contains('operation-item');\n    const isDropTargetTask = this.classList.contains('task-item');\n    const isDropTargetOperation = this.classList.contains('operation-item');\n    const isSameType = (isDraggedTask && isDropTargetTask) || (isDraggedOperation && isDropTargetOperation);\n\n    if (draggedElement !== this && isSameType) {\n        const draggedId = isDraggedTask ? draggedElement.dataset.taskId : draggedElement.dataset.operationId;\n        const dropTargetId = isDropTargetTask ? this.dataset.taskId : this.dataset.operationId;\n\n        console.log(`[DRAG] Valid drop: Moving ${isDraggedTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${draggedId} near ${isDropTargetTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${dropTargetId}`);\n\n        // Get the bounding rectangle of the drop target\n        const rect = this.getBoundingClientRect();\n        const midpoint = rect.top + rect.height / 2;\n\n        // Insert before or after based on mouse position\n        const insertBefore = e.clientY < midpoint;\n        console.log(`[DRAG] Insert position: ${insertBefore ? 'before' : 'after'} drop target`);\n\n        if (insertBefore) {\n            this.parentNode.insertBefore(draggedElement, this);\n        } else {\n            this.parentNode.insertBefore(draggedElement, this.nextSibling);\n        }\n\n        console.log('[DRAG] Element moved in DOM, calling saveOrder()');\n        // Save new order\n        saveOrder(draggedElement);\n    } else {\n        if (draggedElement === this) {\n            console.log('[DRAG] Drop ignored: Element dropped on itself');\n        } else if (!isSameType) {\n            console.log('[DRAG] Drop ignored: Different element types (task vs operation)');\n        }\n    }\n\n    return false;\n}\n\nfunction handleDragEnd(e) {\n    this.classList.remove('dragging');\n\n    // Console tracing for drag end\n    const isTask = this.classList.contains('task-item');\n    const id = isTask ? this.dataset.taskId : this.dataset.operationId;\n    console.log(`[DRAG] End: ${isTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'} ID=${id}`);\n}\n\n/**\n * Save new order after drag and drop\n * Only saves the dragged element's new order position.\n * The backend will recalculate the order for all other elements.\n */\nfunction saveOrder(element) {\n    console.log('[SAVE_ORDER] Function called');\n\n    const isTask = element.classList.contains('task-item');\n    const elementId = isTask ? element.dataset.taskId : element.dataset.operationId;\n    console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Element type: ${isTask ? 'Task' : 'Operation'}, ID: ${elementId}`);\n\n    // Get all siblings of the same type to calculate the new order position\n    const siblings = Array.from(element.parentNode.children).filter(el =>\n        el.classList.contains(isTask ? 'task-item' : 'operation-item')\n    );\n\n    console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Found ${siblings.length} siblings of the same type`);\n\n    // Calculate the new order for the dragged element only\n    const newOrder = siblings.indexOf(element) + 1;\n    console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Dragged element new order: ${newOrder}`);\n\n    // Update the data-order attribute immediately for UI consistency\n    element.dataset.order = newOrder;\n\n    // Send update to server only for the dragged element\n    const formData = new FormData();\n    formData.append('_xsrf', xsrf);\n\n    const url = `https://${window.location.host}/${db}/_m_ord/${elementId}?JSON&order=${newOrder}`;\n    console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Sending API request for ${isTask ? 'task' : 'operation'} ${elementId}: ${url}`);\n\n    fetch(url, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        body: formData\n    })\n    .then(response => {\n        console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] API response for ${isTask ? 'task' : 'operation'} ${elementId}: Status ${response.status}`);\n        return response.json();\n    })\n    .then(data => {\n        console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Order updated for ${isTask ? 'task' : 'operation'} ${elementId}: ${newOrder}`, data);\n        // Reload to show updated order from server (backend recalculates all orders)\n        if (selectedProject) {\n            console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Reloading project details for project ${selectedProject['ПроектID']}`);\n            loadProjectDetails(selectedProject['ПроектID']);\n        }\n    })\n    .catch(error => {\n        console.error(`[SAVE_ORDER] Error updating order for ${isTask ? 'task' : 'operation'} ${elementId}:`, error);\n        alert('Ошибка сохранения порядка');\n        // Reload anyway to restore correct state\n        if (selectedProject) {\n            console.log(`[SAVE_ORDER] Reloading project details after error for project ${selectedProject['ПроектID']}`);\n            loadProjectDetails(selectedProject['ПроектID']);\n        }\n    });\n}\n\n/**\n * Show add project modal\n */\nfunction showAddProjectModal() {\n    document.getElementById('projectModalTitle').textContent = 'Добавить проект';\n    document.getElementById('projectForm').reset();\n    document.getElementById('projectId').value = '';\n    document.getElementById('projectModalBackdrop').classList.add('show');\n}\n\n/**\n * Close project modal\n */\nfunction closeProjectModal() {\n    document.getElementById('projectModalBackdrop').classList.remove('show');\n}\n\n/**\n * Edit project\n */\nfunction editProject() {\n    if (!selectedProject) return;\n\n    document.getElementById('projectModalTitle').textContent = 'Редактировать проект';\n    document.getElementById('projectId').value = selectedProject['ПроектID'];\n    document.getElementById('projectName').value = selectedProject['Проект'] || '';\n    document.getElementById('projectDescription').value = ''; // Not in the project list data\n\n    // Set client if available\n    const clientSelect = document.getElementById('projectClient');\n    const clientOption = Array.from(clientSelect.options).find(opt =>\n        opt.textContent === selectedProject['Заказчик']\n    );\n    if (clientOption) {\n        clientSelect.value = clientOption.value;\n    }\n\n    // Set status if available\n    const statusSelect = document.getElementById('projectStatus');\n    const statusOption = Array.from(statusSelect.options).find(opt =>\n        opt.textContent === selectedProject['Статус проекта']\n    );\n    if (statusOption) {\n        statusSelect.value = statusOption.value;\n    }\n\n    // Set object if available\n    const objectSelect = document.getElementById('projectObject');\n    const objectOption = Array.from(objectSelect.options).find(opt =>\n        opt.textContent === selectedProject['Объект']\n    );\n    if (objectOption) {\n        objectSelect.value = objectOption.value;\n    }\n\n    // Set dates\n    if (selectedProject['Старт']) {\n        document.getElementById('projectStart').value = formatDateForInput(selectedProject['Старт']);\n    }\n    if (selectedProject['Срок']) {\n        document.getElementById('projectDeadline').value = formatDateForInput(selectedProject['Срок']);\n    }\n\n    document.getElementById('projectModalBackdrop').classList.add('show');\n}\n\n/**\n * Show add task modal\n */\nfunction showAddTaskModal() {\n    if (!selectedProject) return;\n\n    document.getElementById('taskModalTitle').textContent = 'Добавить задачу';\n    document.getElementById('taskForm').reset();\n    document.getElementById('taskId').value = '';\n    document.getElementById('taskProjectId').value = selectedProject['ПроектID'];\n    document.getElementById('taskModalBackdrop').classList.add('show');\n}\n\n/**\n * Close task modal\n */\nfunction closeTaskModal() {\n    document.getElementById('taskModalBackdrop').classList.remove('show');\n}\n\n/**\n * Edit task\n */\nfunction editTask(taskId) {\n    const taskData = projectDetails.find(item => item['Задача проектаID'] === taskId);\n    if (!taskData) return;\n\n    document.getElementById('taskModalTitle').textContent = 'Редактировать задачу';\n    document.getElementById('taskId').value = taskId;\n    document.getElementById('taskProjectId').value = selectedProject['ПроектID'];\n    document.getElementById('taskName').value = taskData['Задача проекта'] || '';\n    document.getElementById('taskDescription').value = taskData['Задача Описание'] || '';\n\n    // Set status\n    const statusSelect = document.getElementById('taskStatus');\n    const statusOption =
